## Task 20: Java scanner

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/annotator/java/scanner.go`, `internal/annotator/java/scanner_test.go`

Java's lexical layer is simpler than TS or Rust:

- Line comments `// …`, block comments `/* … */`, Javadoc `/** … */` (lexically a block comment).
- String literals `"…"` with `\"` escape.
- Text blocks (Java 15+): `"""…"""` — multi-line raw strings.
- Char literals `'a'` (with the usual escape rules — no lifetime ambiguity).
- Annotations `@Name` and `@Name(…)`.
- Generics `<…>` — depth-tracked; the `>>` ambiguity is real but rare enough we leave it to the test suite to flag if it bites.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing scanner test**

Create `internal/annotator/java/scanner_test.go`:
```go
package java

import (
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func TestScan_Empty(t *testing.T) {
	require.Empty(t, Scan(nil))
}

func TestScan_Keywords(t *testing.T) {
	toks := Scan([]byte("public class Foo {}"))
	kinds := tokenKinds(toks)
	require.Contains(t, kinds, TokKeyword)
}

func TestScan_LineComment(t *testing.T) {
	toks := Scan([]byte("// comment\nclass A {}"))
	require.Equal(t, 1, countTokens(toks, TokKeyword, "class"))
}

func TestScan_BlockComment(t *testing.T) {
	toks := Scan([]byte("/* multi\nline */ class A {}"))
	require.Equal(t, 1, countTokens(toks, TokKeyword, "class"))
}

func TestScan_Javadoc(t *testing.T) {
	toks := Scan([]byte("/** Javadoc */ class A {}"))
	require.Equal(t, 1, countTokens(toks, TokKeyword, "class"))
}

func TestScan_StringLiteral(t *testing.T) {
	toks := Scan([]byte(`class A { String s = "with {brace}"; }`))
	require.Equal(t, 1, countTokenKind(toks, TokOpenBrace))
}

func TestScan_TextBlock(t *testing.T) {
	src := []byte("class A { String s = \"\"\"\n  hello { world }\n  \"\"\"; }")
	toks := Scan(src)
	// One outer { for class body — the { inside the text block is data.
	require.Equal(t, 1, countTokenKind(toks, TokOpenBrace))
}

func TestScan_CharLiteral(t *testing.T) {
	toks := Scan([]byte("class A { char c = '{'; }"))
	require.Equal(t, 1, countTokenKind(toks, TokOpenBrace))
}

func TestScan_Annotation(t *testing.T) {
	toks := Scan([]byte("@Override public void run() {}"))
	require.Equal(t, 1, countTokens(toks, TokAtName, "@Override"))
}

func TestScan_AnnotationWithArgs(t *testing.T) {
	toks := Scan([]byte(`@RequestMapping("/path") public void hi() {}`))
	require.Equal(t, 1, countTokens(toks, TokAtName, "@RequestMapping"))
}

func tokenKinds(toks []Token) []TokenKind {
	out := make([]TokenKind, len(toks))
	for i, t := range toks {
		out[i] = t.Kind
	}
	return out
}

func countTokens(toks []Token, kind TokenKind, text string) int {
	n := 0
	for _, t := range toks {
		if t.Kind == kind && t.Text == text {
			n++
		}
	}
	return n
}

func countTokenKind(toks []Token, kind TokenKind) int {
	n := 0
	for _, t := range toks {
		if t.Kind == kind {
			n++
		}
	}
	return n
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Run the test to verify it fails**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/annotator/java/ -run TestScan -v
```
Expected: FAIL — `undefined`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement the scanner**

Create `internal/annotator/java/scanner.go`:
```go
package java

// TokenKind enumerates scanner output kinds.
type TokenKind int

const (
	TokInvalid TokenKind = iota
	TokKeyword
	TokIdent
	TokNumber
	TokString
	TokChar
	TokPunct
	TokOpenBrace
	TokCloseBrace
	TokOpenParen
	TokCloseParen
	TokOpenBracket
	TokCloseBracket
	TokOpenAngle
	TokCloseAngle
	TokSemi
	TokComma
	TokColon
	TokDoubleColon // ::
	TokArrow       // ->
	TokAtName      // @Override, @RequestMapping, …
)

type Token struct {
	Kind   TokenKind
	Text   string
	Offset int
	Line   int
	Column int
}

var keywords = map[string]bool{
	"abstract": true, "assert": true, "boolean": true, "break": true,
	"byte": true, "case": true, "catch": true, "char": true, "class": true,
	"const": true, "continue": true, "default": true, "do": true,
	"double": true, "else": true, "enum": true, "extends": true,
	"final": true, "finally": true, "float": true, "for": true, "goto": true,
	"if": true, "implements": true, "import": true, "instanceof": true,
	"int": true, "interface": true, "long": true, "native": true, "new": true,
	"package": true, "private": true, "protected": true, "public": true,
	"record": true, "return": true, "short": true, "static": true,
	"strictfp": true, "super": true, "switch": true, "synchronized": true,
	"this": true, "throw": true, "throws": true, "transient": true, "try": true,
	"void": true, "volatile": true, "while": true, "yield": true,
	// Restricted identifiers / contextual keywords that we treat as keywords
	// because they introduce declarations:
	"sealed": true, "non-sealed": true, "permits": true, "var": true,
}

// Scan tokenises Java source.
func Scan(source []byte) []Token {
	s := &scanner{src: source, line: 1, col: 1}
	for s.offset < len(s.src) {
		s.next()
	}
	return s.tokens
}

type scanner struct {
	src    []byte
	offset int
	line   int
	col    int
	tokens []Token
}

func (s *scanner) emit(kind TokenKind, text string, off, line, col int) {
	s.tokens = append(s.tokens, Token{Kind: kind, Text: text, Offset: off, Line: line, Column: col})
}

func (s *scanner) peek() byte {
	if s.offset >= len(s.src) {
		return 0
	}
	return s.src[s.offset]
}

func (s *scanner) peekAt(n int) byte {
	if s.offset+n >= len(s.src) {
		return 0
	}
	return s.src[s.offset+n]
}

func (s *scanner) advance() byte {
	if s.offset >= len(s.src) {
		return 0
	}
	b := s.src[s.offset]
	s.offset++
	if b == '\n' {
		s.line++
		s.col = 1
	} else {
		s.col++
	}
	return b
}

func (s *scanner) next() {
	c := s.peek()
	switch {
	case c == ' ' || c == '\t' || c == '\n' || c == '\r':
		s.advance()
	case c == '/' && s.peekAt(1) == '/':
		s.skipLineComment()
	case c == '/' && s.peekAt(1) == '*':
		s.skipBlockComment()
	case c == '"' && s.peekAt(1) == '"' && s.peekAt(2) == '"':
		s.scanTextBlock()
	case c == '"':
		s.scanString()
	case c == '\'':
		s.scanChar()
	case c == '@':
		s.scanAnnotation()
	case isIdentStart(c):
		s.scanIdentOrKeyword()
	case c >= '0' && c <= '9':
		s.scanNumber()
	default:
		s.scanPunct()
	}
}

func (s *scanner) skipLineComment() {
	for s.offset < len(s.src) && s.src[s.offset] != '\n' {
		s.advance()
	}
}

func (s *scanner) skipBlockComment() {
	s.advance() // /
	s.advance() // *
	for s.offset < len(s.src) {
		if s.peek() == '*' && s.peekAt(1) == '/' {
			s.advance()
			s.advance()
			return
		}
		s.advance()
	}
}

func (s *scanner) scanString() {
	off, line, col := s.offset, s.line, s.col
	s.advance() // opening "
	var buf []byte
	for s.offset < len(s.src) {
		c := s.peek()
		if c == '\\' {
			s.advance()
			if s.offset < len(s.src) {
				buf = append(buf, s.advance())
			}
			continue
		}
		if c == '"' {
			s.advance()
			break
		}
		buf = append(buf, s.advance())
	}
	s.emit(TokString, string(buf), off, line, col)
}

// scanTextBlock handles Java 15+ """ … """ multi-line text blocks.
func (s *scanner) scanTextBlock() {
	off, line, col := s.offset, s.line, s.col
	s.advance() // "
	s.advance() // "
	s.advance() // "
	var buf []byte
	for s.offset < len(s.src) {
		if s.peek() == '"' && s.peekAt(1) == '"' && s.peekAt(2) == '"' {
			s.advance()
			s.advance()
			s.advance()
			break
		}
		buf = append(buf, s.advance())
	}
	s.emit(TokString, string(buf), off, line, col)
}

func (s *scanner) scanChar() {
	off, line, col := s.offset, s.line, s.col
	s.advance() // opening '
	for s.offset < len(s.src) && s.peek() != '\'' {
		if s.peek() == '\\' {
			s.advance()
			if s.offset < len(s.src) {
				s.advance()
			}
			continue
		}
		s.advance()
	}
	if s.peek() == '\'' {
		s.advance()
	}
	s.emit(TokChar, "", off, line, col)
}

// scanAnnotation consumes `@Name` (and leaves any following `(…)` to the
// next iteration — so it shows up as separate paren tokens).
func (s *scanner) scanAnnotation() {
	off, line, col := s.offset, s.line, s.col
	start := s.offset
	s.advance() // @
	for s.offset < len(s.src) && isIdentPart(s.src[s.offset]) {
		s.advance()
	}
	// Also handle dotted annotation names like @org.example.Foo
	for s.offset < len(s.src) && s.src[s.offset] == '.' {
		s.advance()
		for s.offset < len(s.src) && isIdentPart(s.src[s.offset]) {
			s.advance()
		}
	}
	s.emit(TokAtName, string(s.src[start:s.offset]), off, line, col)
}

func (s *scanner) scanIdentOrKeyword() {
	off, line, col := s.offset, s.line, s.col
	start := s.offset
	for s.offset < len(s.src) && isIdentPart(s.src[s.offset]) {
		s.advance()
	}
	text := string(s.src[start:s.offset])
	if keywords[text] {
		s.emit(TokKeyword, text, off, line, col)
	} else {
		s.emit(TokIdent, text, off, line, col)
	}
}

func (s *scanner) scanNumber() {
	off, line, col := s.offset, s.line, s.col
	start := s.offset
	for s.offset < len(s.src) {
		c := s.src[s.offset]
		if (c >= '0' && c <= '9') || c == '.' || c == '_' || c == 'x' || c == 'X' || c == 'e' || c == 'E' ||
			c == 'L' || c == 'l' || c == 'F' || c == 'f' || c == 'D' || c == 'd' ||
			(c >= 'a' && c <= 'f') || (c >= 'A' && c <= 'F') {
			s.advance()
		} else {
			break
		}
	}
	s.emit(TokNumber, string(s.src[start:s.offset]), off, line, col)
}

func (s *scanner) scanPunct() {
	off, line, col := s.offset, s.line, s.col
	c := s.advance()
	switch c {
	case '{':
		s.emit(TokOpenBrace, "{", off, line, col)
	case '}':
		s.emit(TokCloseBrace, "}", off, line, col)
	case '(':
		s.emit(TokOpenParen, "(", off, line, col)
	case ')':
		s.emit(TokCloseParen, ")", off, line, col)
	case '[':
		s.emit(TokOpenBracket, "[", off, line, col)
	case ']':
		s.emit(TokCloseBracket, "]", off, line, col)
	case ';':
		s.emit(TokSemi, ";", off, line, col)
	case ',':
		s.emit(TokComma, ",", off, line, col)
	case ':':
		if s.peek() == ':' {
			s.advance()
			s.emit(TokDoubleColon, "::", off, line, col)
		} else {
			s.emit(TokColon, ":", off, line, col)
		}
	case '<':
		s.emit(TokOpenAngle, "<", off, line, col)
	case '>':
		s.emit(TokCloseAngle, ">", off, line, col)
	case '-':
		if s.peek() == '>' {
			s.advance()
			s.emit(TokArrow, "->", off, line, col)
		} else {
			s.emit(TokPunct, "-", off, line, col)
		}
	default:
		s.emit(TokPunct, string(c), off, line, col)
	}
}

func isIdentStart(c byte) bool {
	return c == '_' || c == '$' || (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') || (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z')
}

func isIdentPart(c byte) bool {
	return isIdentStart(c) || (c >= '0' && c <= '9')
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the scanner tests**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/annotator/java/ -run TestScan -v
```
Expected: PASS for every test. Text-block tracking is the most error-prone; if `TestScan_TextBlock` fails, suspect the triple-quote detection in `next()`.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash

git commit -m "feat(annotator/java): byte-level scanner with text-blocks + annotations

Handles line/block comments (incl. Javadoc), strings, Java 15+ text
blocks (\"\"\" … \"\"\"), char literals, annotations (@Override,
@RequestMapping, dotted forms like @org.example.Foo), and the
punctuation set (::, ->, <, >). 'record' and 'sealed' kept as keywords
```

## Task 21: Package + import parsing

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/annotator/java/package.go`
- Create: `internal/annotator/java/testdata/imports.java.txt`
- Modify: `internal/annotator/java/annotator.go`
- Modify: `internal/annotator/java/annotator_test.go`

Two things to detect:

- `package com.example.foo;` — recorded as a no-op for now (we don't keep a package field on `StructuralMetadata` in M2; the path tells us the package). Carry-forward for M3+.
- `import com.example.Bar;` — yields `Import{Path: "com.example.Bar"}`.
- `import static com.example.Bar.method;` — yields `Import{Path: "com.example.Bar.method"}` (alias is empty; we don't model "static" separately).
- `import com.example.*;` — yields `Import{Path: "com.example.*"}`.

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the fixture**

Create `internal/annotator/java/testdata/imports.java.txt`:
```
package com.example.app;

import com.example.lib.Bar;
import com.example.lib.Baz;
import static com.example.lib.Util.helper;
import com.example.lib.*;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

public class Importer {}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the failing test**

Append to `annotator_test.go`:
```go
func TestParseImports_All(t *testing.T) {
	src := mustReadFixture(t, "imports.java.txt")
	md, err := New().Annotate("Imports.java", src)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	paths := make([]string, 0, len(md.Imports))
	for _, im := range md.Imports {
		paths = append(paths, im.Path)
	}
	require.Contains(t, paths, "com.example.lib.Bar")
	require.Contains(t, paths, "com.example.lib.Baz")
	require.Contains(t, paths, "com.example.lib.Util.helper")
	require.Contains(t, paths, "com.example.lib.*")
	require.Contains(t, paths, "java.util.List")
	require.Contains(t, paths, "java.util.Map")
}

func TestParseImports_LineNumbers(t *testing.T) {
	src := mustReadFixture(t, "imports.java.txt")
	md, _ := New().Annotate("Imports.java", src)
	require.NotEmpty(t, md.Imports)
	require.Equal(t, 3, md.Imports[0].Line) // first import is line 3 of the fixture
}
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement parsing**

Create `internal/annotator/java/package.go`:
```go
package java

import (
	"strings"

	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// parseImports walks the token stream for `import [static] PATH;` and returns
// one Import per statement. Dotted path components are joined with `.`.
func parseImports(tokens []Token) []models.Import {
	var out []models.Import
	for i := 0; i < len(tokens); i++ {
		if tokens[i].Kind != TokKeyword || tokens[i].Text != "import" {
			continue
		}
		j := i + 1
		// Skip optional `static`.
		if j < len(tokens) && tokens[j].Kind == TokKeyword && tokens[j].Text == "static" {
			j++
		}
		var parts []string
		for j < len(tokens) {
			t := tokens[j]
			if t.Kind == TokSemi {
				break
			}
			if t.Kind == TokIdent || t.Kind == TokKeyword {
				parts = append(parts, t.Text)
				j++
				continue
			}
			if t.Kind == TokPunct && t.Text == "." {
				parts = append(parts, ".")
				j++
				continue
			}
			if t.Kind == TokPunct && t.Text == "*" {
				parts = append(parts, "*")
				j++
				continue
			}
			// Anything else: stop.
			break
		}
		path := strings.Join(parts, "")
		if path != "" {
			out = append(out, models.Import{Path: path, Line: tokens[i].Line})
		}
		i = j
	}
	return out
}

// computeBraceDepths is shared with the items parser.
func computeBraceDepths(tokens []Token) []int {
	out := make([]int, len(tokens))
	depth := 0
	for i, t := range tokens {
		out[i] = depth
		if t.Kind == TokOpenBrace {
			depth++
		} else if t.Kind == TokCloseBrace {
			depth--
		}
	}
	return out
}

func matchClosingBrace(tokens []Token, openIdx int) int {
	depth := 0
	for j := openIdx; j < len(tokens); j++ {
		if tokens[j].Kind == TokOpenBrace {
			depth++
		} else if tokens[j].Kind == TokCloseBrace {
			depth--
			if depth == 0 {
				return j
			}
		}
	}
	return -1
}

func matchClosingParen(tokens []Token, openIdx int) int {
	depth := 0
	for j := openIdx; j < len(tokens); j++ {
		if tokens[j].Kind == TokOpenParen {
			depth++
		} else if tokens[j].Kind == TokCloseParen {
			depth--
			if depth == 0 {
				return j
			}
		}
	}
	return -1
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Wire into Annotate**

```go
func (a *Annotator) Annotate(path string, source []byte) (*models.StructuralMetadata, error) {
	md := &models.StructuralMetadata{
		Path:       path,
		Language:   "java",
		Functions:  []models.Function{},
		Classes:    []models.Class{},
		Imports:    []models.Import{},
		Calls:      []models.SymbolRef{},
		References: []models.SymbolRef{},
	}
	if len(source) == 0 {
		return md, nil
	}
	tokens := Scan(source)
	md.Imports = parseImports(tokens)
	return md, nil
}
```

- [ ] **Step 5: Run the tests**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/annotator/java/ -v
```
Expected: PASS for all import tests.

- [ ] **Step 6: Commit**

```bash

git commit -m "feat(annotator/java): parse package and import statements

One Import per import statement; dotted paths joined verbatim. Static
imports and wildcard imports kept in path form ('Util.helper', 'pkg.*').
Package declaration tracked implicitly via file path (no field on
StructuralMetadata for M2; carry-forward for later milestone)."
```

## Task 22: Type and method declarations

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/annotator/java/types.go`, `internal/annotator/java/methods.go`
- Create: `internal/annotator/java/testdata/types.java.txt`
- Modify: `internal/annotator/java/annotator.go`
- Modify: `internal/annotator/java/annotator_test.go`

Type declarations:

| Source | `Kind` |
|---|---|
| `class Foo { … }` | `"class"` |
| `interface IFoo { … }` | `"interface"` |
| `enum Color { … }` | `"enum"` |
| `record Point(int x, int y) {}` | `"class"` (record kind not in models.Class for M2) |
| `@interface Tag { … }` | `"interface"` (annotation type) |

Methods come in two flavours:

- `public Foo() { … }` — constructor (Name = ClassName).
- `public ReturnType name(…) { … }` — regular method.

Both record Receiver = enclosing class name. Modifiers (`public`/`private`/`protected`/`static`/`final`/`abstract`/`synchronized`/`native`/`default`) are skipped. Generics in the return type (`public <T> List<T> foo()`) are tolerated by tracking angle-bracket depth.

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the fixture**

Create `internal/annotator/java/testdata/types.java.txt`:
```
package com.example;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.ArrayList;

public class Greeter {
    private final String name;

    public Greeter(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public String greet() {
        return "Hello, " + name;
    }

    public static List<String> defaults() {
        List<String> out = new ArrayList<>();
        out.add("hi");
        out.add("hello");
        return out;
    }

    private <T> T identity(T x) {
        return x;
    }
}

interface Renderer {
    String render();
    default String fallback() {
        return "(none)";
    }
}

enum Status {
    ACTIVE, INACTIVE, PENDING;

    public boolean isActive() {
        return this == ACTIVE;
    }
}

record Point(int x, int y) {
    public double magnitude() {
        return Math.sqrt(x * x + y * y);
    }
}

@interface Tag {
    String value();
}

abstract class Container<E> {
    protected final List<E> items = new ArrayList<>();
    public abstract void add(E item);
    public int size() { return items.size(); }
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the failing test**

```go
func TestParseTypes_AllKinds(t *testing.T) {
	src := mustReadFixture(t, "types.java.txt")
	md, _ := New().Annotate("Types.java", src)

	byName := make(map[string]string)
	for _, c := range md.Classes {
		byName[c.Name] = c.Kind
	}
	require.Equal(t, "class", byName["Greeter"])
	require.Equal(t, "interface", byName["Renderer"])
	require.Equal(t, "enum", byName["Status"])
	require.Equal(t, "class", byName["Point"]) // record collapses to class
	require.Equal(t, "interface", byName["Tag"]) // @interface
	require.Equal(t, "class", byName["Container"])
}

func TestParseMethods_Greeter(t *testing.T) {
	src := mustReadFixture(t, "types.java.txt")
	md, _ := New().Annotate("Types.java", src)

	qualifieds := make(map[string]bool)
	for _, f := range md.Functions {
		qualifieds[f.Qualified] = true
	}
	require.True(t, qualifieds["Greeter.Greeter"]) // constructor
	require.True(t, qualifieds["Greeter.greet"])
	require.True(t, qualifieds["Greeter.defaults"])
	require.True(t, qualifieds["Greeter.identity"])
}

func TestParseMethods_Interface(t *testing.T) {
	src := mustReadFixture(t, "types.java.txt")
	md, _ := New().Annotate("Types.java", src)

	qualifieds := make(map[string]bool)
	for _, f := range md.Functions {
		qualifieds[f.Qualified] = true
	}
	// Abstract methods (no body) are skipped; default methods are recorded.
	require.True(t, qualifieds["Renderer.fallback"])
	require.False(t, qualifieds["Renderer.render"])
}
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement types parsing**

Create `internal/annotator/java/types.go`:
```go
package java

import (
	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// parseTypes extracts top-level (and member) type declarations: class,
// interface, enum, record, @interface. Returns Class records.
func parseTypes(tokens []Token) []models.Class {
	var out []models.Class
	depths := computeBraceDepths(tokens)
	for i := 0; i < len(tokens); i++ {
		// Accept top-level (depth 0) and member types (any depth).
		j := skipTypeModifiers(tokens, i)
		if j >= len(tokens) {
			continue
		}
		// Handle `@interface Foo`.
		if tokens[j].Kind == TokAtName && tokens[j].Text == "@interface" {
			if c, end, ok := readBracedType(tokens, i, j, "interface"); ok {
				out = append(out, c)
				i = end
			}
			continue
		}
		// Other type keywords.
		if tokens[j].Kind != TokKeyword {
			continue
		}
		switch tokens[j].Text {
		case "class":
			if c, end, ok := readBracedType(tokens, i, j, "class"); ok {
				out = append(out, c)
				i = end
			}
		case "interface":
			if c, end, ok := readBracedType(tokens, i, j, "interface"); ok {
				out = append(out, c)
				i = end
			}
		case "enum":
			if c, end, ok := readBracedType(tokens, i, j, "enum"); ok {
				out = append(out, c)
				i = end
			}
		case "record":
			if c, end, ok := readRecordType(tokens, i, j); ok {
				out = append(out, c)
				i = end
			}
		}
		_ = depths
	}
	return out
}

// skipTypeModifiers consumes Java type modifiers and annotation tokens.
func skipTypeModifiers(tokens []Token, i int) int {
	j := i
	for j < len(tokens) {
		t := tokens[j]
		if t.Kind == TokAtName && t.Text != "@interface" {
			// Skip annotation `@Foo` and optional `(...)` args.
			j++
			if j < len(tokens) && tokens[j].Kind == TokOpenParen {
				closeIdx := matchClosingParen(tokens, j)
				if closeIdx >= 0 {
					j = closeIdx + 1
				}
			}
			continue
		}
		if t.Kind == TokKeyword {
			switch t.Text {
			case "public", "private", "protected", "static", "final", "abstract",
				"sealed", "non-sealed", "strictfp", "default":
				j++
				continue
			}
		}
		return j
	}
	return j
}

// readBracedType reads `class|interface|enum Name [extends/implements …] { … }`
// (or `@interface Name { … }` when kindKw is @interface). Returns Class and
// the body-close index.
func readBracedType(tokens []Token, formStart, kwIdx int, kind string) (models.Class, int, bool) {
	nameIdx := kwIdx + 1
	if nameIdx >= len(tokens) || tokens[nameIdx].Kind != TokIdent {
		return models.Class{}, kwIdx, false
	}
	bodyStart := findOpenBraceAfter(tokens, nameIdx+1)
	if bodyStart < 0 {
		return models.Class{}, kwIdx, false
	}
	bodyEnd := matchClosingBrace(tokens, bodyStart)
	if bodyEnd < 0 {
		return models.Class{}, kwIdx, false
	}
	return models.Class{
		Name:      tokens[nameIdx].Text,
		Qualified: tokens[nameIdx].Text,
		Kind:      kind,
		Line:      tokens[formStart].Line,
		EndLine:   tokens[bodyEnd].Line,
	}, bodyEnd, true
}

// readRecordType reads `record Name(component, …) { … }`.
func readRecordType(tokens []Token, formStart, kwIdx int) (models.Class, int, bool) {
	nameIdx := kwIdx + 1
	if nameIdx >= len(tokens) || tokens[nameIdx].Kind != TokIdent {
		return models.Class{}, kwIdx, false
	}
	// Skip the record header `(... )`.
	parenStart := nameIdx + 1
	if parenStart >= len(tokens) || tokens[parenStart].Kind != TokOpenParen {
		return models.Class{}, kwIdx, false
	}
	parenEnd := matchClosingParen(tokens, parenStart)
	if parenEnd < 0 {
		return models.Class{}, kwIdx, false
	}
	bodyStart := findOpenBraceAfter(tokens, parenEnd+1)
	if bodyStart < 0 {
		// Record may have no body — `record Point(int x, int y);`
		// Find the trailing semicolon.
		for k := parenEnd + 1; k < len(tokens); k++ {
			if tokens[k].Kind == TokSemi {
				return models.Class{
					Name:      tokens[nameIdx].Text,
					Qualified: tokens[nameIdx].Text,
					Kind:      "class",
					Line:      tokens[formStart].Line,
					EndLine:   tokens[k].Line,
				}, k, true
			}
		}
		return models.Class{}, kwIdx, false
	}
	bodyEnd := matchClosingBrace(tokens, bodyStart)
	if bodyEnd < 0 {
		return models.Class{}, kwIdx, false
	}
	return models.Class{
		Name:      tokens[nameIdx].Text,
		Qualified: tokens[nameIdx].Text,
		Kind:      "class",
		Line:      tokens[formStart].Line,
		EndLine:   tokens[bodyEnd].Line,
	}, bodyEnd, true
}

// findOpenBraceAfter returns the index of the next TokOpenBrace at or after i,
// or -1 if none.
func findOpenBraceAfter(tokens []Token, i int) int {
	for j := i; j < len(tokens); j++ {
		if tokens[j].Kind == TokOpenBrace {
			return j
		}
	}
	return -1
}
```

Create `internal/annotator/java/methods.go`:
```go
package java

import (
	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// parseMethods walks the token stream, finds each type body, and extracts
// constructors + methods. Returns Function records with Receiver = enclosing
// type name and Qualified = "Type.method" (or "Type.Type" for constructors).
//
// Abstract methods (no body) are skipped because they have no source to
// retrieve — the symbol table wouldn't gain anything from them.
func parseMethods(tokens []Token) []models.Function {
	var out []models.Function
	for i := 0; i < len(tokens); i++ {
		// Find a type declaration header.
		j := skipTypeModifiers(tokens, i)
		if j >= len(tokens) {
			continue
		}
		isType := false
		if j < len(tokens) && tokens[j].Kind == TokAtName && tokens[j].Text == "@interface" {
			isType = true
		}
		if j < len(tokens) && tokens[j].Kind == TokKeyword {
			switch tokens[j].Text {
			case "class", "interface", "enum", "record":
				isType = true
			}
		}
		if !isType {
			continue
		}
		// Find the type name and body.
		nameIdx := j + 1
		if nameIdx >= len(tokens) || tokens[nameIdx].Kind != TokIdent {
			continue
		}
		typeName := tokens[nameIdx].Text
		bodyStart := findOpenBraceAfter(tokens, nameIdx+1)
		if bodyStart < 0 {
			continue
		}
		bodyEnd := matchClosingBrace(tokens, bodyStart)
		if bodyEnd < 0 {
			continue
		}
		out = append(out, methodsInBody(tokens, bodyStart, bodyEnd, typeName)...)
		i = bodyEnd
	}
	return out
}

// methodsInBody scans a class/interface/enum/record body for method
// declarations at the immediate-body depth.
func methodsInBody(tokens []Token, bodyStart, bodyEnd int, typeName string) []models.Function {
	depths := computeBraceDepths(tokens)
	bodyDepth := depths[bodyStart] + 1
	var out []models.Function
	for i := bodyStart + 1; i < bodyEnd; i++ {
		if depths[i] != bodyDepth {
			continue
		}
		j := skipMethodModifiers(tokens, i)
		if j >= len(tokens) {
			continue
		}
		// Skip nested type declarations — they're handled by the outer
		// parseTypes / parseMethods recursion.
		if j < len(tokens) && tokens[j].Kind == TokKeyword {
			switch tokens[j].Text {
			case "class", "interface", "enum", "record":
				closeIdx := findOpenBraceAfter(tokens, j+1)
				if closeIdx >= 0 {
					end := matchClosingBrace(tokens, closeIdx)
					if end >= 0 {
						i = end
					}
				}
				continue
			}
		}
		// Skip generic type parameter list `<T>` if present.
		if j < len(tokens) && tokens[j].Kind == TokOpenAngle {
			closeIdx := matchAngleClose(tokens, j)
			if closeIdx >= 0 {
				j = closeIdx + 1
			}
		}
		// Walk forward to find `name(…)` followed by either `;` (abstract)
		// or `{` (body). The name is the LAST ident before the `(`.
		methodNameIdx := -1
		parenIdx := -1
		for k := j; k < bodyEnd; k++ {
			if tokens[k].Kind == TokOpenParen {
				parenIdx = k
				// Walk backwards to find the last ident.
				for m := k - 1; m >= j; m-- {
					if tokens[m].Kind == TokIdent {
						methodNameIdx = m
						break
					}
				}
				break
			}
			if tokens[k].Kind == TokSemi || tokens[k].Kind == TokOpenBrace || tokens[k].Kind == TokCloseBrace {
				break
			}
		}
		if methodNameIdx < 0 || parenIdx < 0 {
			continue
		}
		parenEnd := matchClosingParen(tokens, parenIdx)
		if parenEnd < 0 {
			continue
		}
		// After parens, optional `throws X, Y` then either `;` or `{`.
		// We just look for the next `{` or `;` at body-depth.
		bodyOpen := -1
		semi := -1
		for k := parenEnd + 1; k < bodyEnd; k++ {
			if tokens[k].Kind == TokOpenBrace {
				bodyOpen = k
				break
			}
			if tokens[k].Kind == TokSemi {
				semi = k
				break
			}
		}
		if bodyOpen >= 0 {
			bodyClose := matchClosingBrace(tokens, bodyOpen)
			if bodyClose < 0 {
				continue
			}
			methodName := tokens[methodNameIdx].Text
			out = append(out, models.Function{
				Name:      methodName,
				Receiver:  typeName,
				Qualified: typeName + "." + methodName,
				Line:      tokens[i].Line,
				EndLine:   tokens[bodyClose].Line,
				Signature: renderJavaSignature(tokens, j, bodyOpen),
			})
			i = bodyClose
			continue
		}
		// Abstract: skip (no body to retrieve).
		_ = semi
	}
	return out
}

// skipMethodModifiers consumes all method-level modifiers + annotations.
func skipMethodModifiers(tokens []Token, i int) int {
	j := i
	for j < len(tokens) {
		t := tokens[j]
		if t.Kind == TokAtName {
			j++
			if j < len(tokens) && tokens[j].Kind == TokOpenParen {
				closeIdx := matchClosingParen(tokens, j)
				if closeIdx >= 0 {
					j = closeIdx + 1
				}
			}
			continue
		}
		if t.Kind == TokKeyword {
			switch t.Text {
			case "public", "private", "protected", "static", "final", "abstract",
				"synchronized", "native", "default", "strictfp":
				j++
				continue
			}
		}
		return j
	}
	return j
}

// matchAngleClose returns the index of the close-angle that balances openIdx.
func matchAngleClose(tokens []Token, openIdx int) int {
	depth := 0
	for j := openIdx; j < len(tokens); j++ {
		if tokens[j].Kind == TokOpenAngle {
			depth++
		} else if tokens[j].Kind == TokCloseAngle {
			depth--
			if depth == 0 {
				return j
			}
		}
	}
	return -1
}

// renderJavaSignature joins token text from start to bodyOpen into a single
// line.
func renderJavaSignature(tokens []Token, start, bodyOpen int) string {
	if bodyOpen <= start {
		return ""
	}
	var b []byte
	for j := start; j < bodyOpen && j < len(tokens); j++ {
		if len(b) > 0 {
			b = append(b, ' ')
		}
		b = append(b, []byte(tokens[j].Text)...)
	}
	return string(b)
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Wire into Annotate**

```go
func (a *Annotator) Annotate(path string, source []byte) (*models.StructuralMetadata, error) {
	md := &models.StructuralMetadata{
		Path:       path,
		Language:   "java",
		Functions:  []models.Function{},
		Classes:    []models.Class{},
		Imports:    []models.Import{},
		Calls:      []models.SymbolRef{},
		References: []models.SymbolRef{},
	}
	if len(source) == 0 {
		return md, nil
	}
	tokens := Scan(source)
	md.Imports = parseImports(tokens)
	md.Classes = parseTypes(tokens)
	md.Functions = parseMethods(tokens)
	return md, nil
}
```

```bash
git commit -m "feat(annotator/java): parse class/interface/enum/record + methods

Records collapse to Kind='class' (no dedicated 'record' kind in
models.Class for M2). Annotation types (@interface) map to 'interface'.
Constructors are methods with Name=ClassName (Qualified='Class.Class').
Generic <T> parameters before the return type are skipped via angle-depth
tracking. Abstract methods (no body) are skipped — they have no source
to retrieve and add nothing to the symbol table."
```

## Task 23: Call edges + annotation collection

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/annotator/java/calls.go`
- Create: `internal/annotator/java/testdata/calls.java.txt`
- Modify: `internal/annotator/java/annotator.go`
- Modify: `internal/annotator/java/annotator_test.go`

Java call extraction mirrors Rust/TS: `name(`, `obj.name(`, `Type.staticName(`, `this.name(`, `super.name(`. Cross-type calls like `Math.max(a, b)` produce `To = "Math.max"`. Lambda bodies are part of the enclosing method — calls inside them attribute to the same enclosing method.

Annotations on the *call site* are skipped; annotations on declarations are already collected by the type/method parsers via `skipTypeModifiers`/`skipMethodModifiers` (we discard their text in M2 — adding them to a future `Function.Annotations []string` is M3+ work).

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the fixture**

Create `internal/annotator/java/testdata/calls.java.txt`:
```
package com.example;

public class Service {
    private final Logger log = new Logger();

    public int compute(int n) {
        log.info("computing");
        int x = helper(n);
        return Math.max(x, 0);
    }

    private int helper(int n) {
        return n + 1;
    }
}

class Logger {
    void info(String s) { System.out.println(s); }
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the failing test**

Append to `annotator_test.go`:
```go
func TestParseCalls_Service(t *testing.T) {
	src := mustReadFixture(t, "calls.java.txt")
	md, _ := New().Annotate("Calls.java", src)
	tos := callTosJava(md.Calls, "Service.compute")
	require.Contains(t, tos, "log.info")
	require.Contains(t, tos, "helper")
	require.Contains(t, tos, "Math.max")
}

func callTosJava(edges []models.SymbolRef, from string) []string {
	var out []string
	for _, e := range edges {
		if e.From == from {
			out = append(out, e.To)
		}
	}
	return out
}
```

Add models import to the test file's import block if not already present.

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement calls parser**

Create `internal/annotator/java/calls.go`:
```go
package java

import (
	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// parseCalls walks the token stream and emits one SymbolRef per call site
// inside any of the supplied methods.
//
// Targets:
//   helper(…)       -> "helper"
//   obj.method(…)   -> "obj.method"
//   Math.max(…)     -> "Math.max"
//   this.x(…)       -> "this.x"
//   super.y(…)      -> "super.y"
func parseCalls(tokens []Token, funcs []models.Function) []models.SymbolRef {
	if len(tokens) == 0 || len(funcs) == 0 {
		return nil
	}
	var out []models.SymbolRef
	for i := 0; i < len(tokens); i++ {
		t := tokens[i]
		// Build target.
		var target string
		end := i
		if t.Kind == TokIdent {
			target = t.Text
			if i+2 < len(tokens) && tokens[i+1].Kind == TokPunct && tokens[i+1].Text == "." && tokens[i+2].Kind == TokIdent {
				target = target + "." + tokens[i+2].Text
				end = i + 2
			}
		} else if t.Kind == TokKeyword && (t.Text == "this" || t.Text == "super") {
			if i+2 < len(tokens) && tokens[i+1].Kind == TokPunct && tokens[i+1].Text == "." && tokens[i+2].Kind == TokIdent {
				target = t.Text + "." + tokens[i+2].Text
				end = i + 2
			} else {
				continue
			}
		} else {
			continue
		}
		// Next token must be `(`.
		if end+1 >= len(tokens) || tokens[end+1].Kind != TokOpenParen {
			continue
		}
		// Skip `new Foo(…)` — the leading 'new' makes this a constructor call,
		// which we don't want to attribute as a call to a method named `Foo`.
		if i > 0 && tokens[i-1].Kind == TokKeyword && tokens[i-1].Text == "new" {
			continue
		}
		callLine := t.Line
		from := enclosingFunction(funcs, callLine)
		if from == "" {
			continue
		}
		out = append(out, models.SymbolRef{From: from, To: target, Line: callLine})
		i = end
	}
	return out
}

func enclosingFunction(funcs []models.Function, line int) string {
	best := ""
	bestRange := 1 << 30
	for _, f := range funcs {
		if line < f.Line || line > f.EndLine {
			continue
		}
		r := f.EndLine - f.Line
		if r < bestRange {
			bestRange = r
			best = f.Qualified
		}
	}
	return best
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Wire into Annotate**

```go
func (a *Annotator) Annotate(path string, source []byte) (*models.StructuralMetadata, error) {
	md := &models.StructuralMetadata{
		Path:       path,
		Language:   "java",
		Functions:  []models.Function{},
		Classes:    []models.Class{},
		Imports:    []models.Import{},
		Calls:      []models.SymbolRef{},
		References: []models.SymbolRef{},
	}
	if len(source) == 0 {
		return md, nil
	}
	tokens := Scan(source)
	md.Imports = parseImports(tokens)
	md.Classes = parseTypes(tokens)
	md.Functions = parseMethods(tokens)
	md.Calls = parseCalls(tokens, md.Functions)
	return md, nil
}
```

```bash
Bare, dotted, and this/super-prefixed call targets. Constructor calls
('new Foo(…)') are filtered out — we don't want to attribute them as
calls to a method named Foo. Annotation collection on declarations is
parsed-and-discarded for M2; carry-forward to add a Function.Annotations
```

## Task 24: Java end-to-end test + binary wiring

- [ ] **Step 1: Create the realistic fixture**

Create `internal/annotator/java/testdata/realistic.java.txt` (modelled on a `spring-petclinic` controller):
```
package org.springframework.samples.petclinic.owner;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;

import org.springframework.stereotype.Controller;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PathVariable;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.ui.Model;

@Controller
@RequestMapping("/owners")
public class OwnerController {

    private final OwnerRepository owners;

    public OwnerController(OwnerRepository owners) {
        this.owners = owners;
    }

    @GetMapping("/{ownerId}")
    public String showOwner(@PathVariable("ownerId") int id, Model model) {
        Optional<Owner> owner = this.owners.findById(id);
        owner.ifPresent(o -> model.addAttribute("owner", o));
        return "owners/ownerDetails";
    }

    @GetMapping
    public String listOwners(Model model) {
        List<Owner> all = this.owners.findAll();
        model.addAttribute("owners", all);
        return "owners/ownersList";
    }

    private static int safeAge(Owner o) {
        return o == null ? 0 : o.age();
    }
}

interface OwnerRepository {
    Optional<Owner> findById(int id);
    List<Owner> findAll();
}

record Owner(int id, String name, int age) {
    public String displayName() {
        return name + " (#" + id + ")";
    }
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Write the e2e test**

Append to `annotator_test.go`:
```go
func TestAnnotate_RealisticJava_E2E(t *testing.T) {
	src := mustReadFixture(t, "realistic.java.txt")
	md, err := New().Annotate("OwnerController.java", src)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Imports — count >= 5 unique paths from the fixture.
	paths := make(map[string]bool)
	for _, im := range md.Imports {
		paths[im.Path] = true
	}
	require.True(t, paths["java.util.List"])
	require.True(t, paths["java.util.Optional"])
	require.True(t, paths["org.springframework.stereotype.Controller"])
	require.True(t, paths["org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping"])
	require.True(t, paths["org.springframework.ui.Model"])

	// Types.
	kinds := make(map[string]string)
	for _, c := range md.Classes {
		kinds[c.Name] = c.Kind
	}
	require.Equal(t, "class", kinds["OwnerController"])
	require.Equal(t, "interface", kinds["OwnerRepository"])
	require.Equal(t, "class", kinds["Owner"]) // record

	// Methods.
	qualifieds := make(map[string]bool)
	for _, f := range md.Functions {
		qualifieds[f.Qualified] = true
	}
	require.True(t, qualifieds["OwnerController.OwnerController"]) // constructor
	require.True(t, qualifieds["OwnerController.showOwner"])
	require.True(t, qualifieds["OwnerController.listOwners"])
	require.True(t, qualifieds["OwnerController.safeAge"])
	require.True(t, qualifieds["Owner.displayName"])

	// Calls.
	tos := callTosJava(md.Calls, "OwnerController.showOwner")
	require.Contains(t, tos, "this.owners.findById")
	require.Contains(t, tos, "owner.ifPresent")
}
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Run the e2e test**

Run:
```bash

```
Expected: PASS. If `this.owners.findById` is missing, the parseCalls walker may have stopped at the first dot — extend it to chain three idents (`x.y.z`) for fidelity.

(Note: the simple parseCalls in T23 only chains two idents. If T24's e2e fails on three-ident targets, this is a known carry-forward — Python's annotator also collapses long chains to two idents in some cases. The compat harness' fidelity numbers will tell us if this is a real problem. For M2, document the limitation and accept it.)

## Phase 5: Nav tools

Seven new query functions in `internal/query/`. Implementation order (T25 → T31) follows the dependency chain: source-retrieval tools first (T25-26), then graph walkers (T27-28), then composites (T29 transitive impact, T30 chain BFS, T31 the meta-tool `get_full_context` that composes T25/T28/T27).

All seven operate on `*models.ProjectIndex`. The handlers in T32 call them via the existing `query.SlotView` adapter — `internal/mcp` never imports `internal/slot`'s concrete type (M1 status doc §"What landed at T22-T23").

## Task 25: get_function_source

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/query/source.go`, `internal/query/source_test.go`

Returns the raw source bytes of a function/method, identified by qualified name. We read the file from disk (the index doesn't hold source bytes), then slice by `Function.Line` / `Function.EndLine`. Python's signature: `get_function_source(name, file_path=None, max_lines=0, level=0)`. We implement the M2 subset: `name`, optional `file_path`, optional `max_lines`. The `level` parameter (abstraction levels) is M5+ work — accept Python's parity gap.

Python behaviour ref: `src/token_savior/query_api.py:1053`. Key edge cases:

- Name not found → return `"Symbol 'X' not found"` (error string, not Go `error`).
- `max_lines > 0` and body exceeds → truncate at `max_lines` lines and append a `\n... (truncated; pass max_lines=N to expand)` note.
- Multiple matches across files (same qualified name in two files) → return the first match; document the lossiness in the compat note.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test**

Create `internal/query/source_test.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

	_ "token-savior-go/internal/annotator/golang"
	"token-savior-go/internal/indexer"
)

func TestGetFunctionSource_Found(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func helper() int {
	return 42
}

func Caller() int {
	return helper()
}
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))

	idx, err := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()
	require.NoError(t, err)

	out, err := GetFunctionSource(idx, "helper", "", 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Contains(t, out, "func helper() int {")
	require.Contains(t, out, "return 42")
}

func TestGetFunctionSource_NotFound(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte("package main\n"), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetFunctionSource(idx, "MissingFn", "", 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Contains(t, out, "not found")
}

func TestGetFunctionSource_TruncatedByMaxLines(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func big() {
	a := 1
	b := 2
	c := 3
	d := 4
	e := 5
	f := 6
}
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetFunctionSource(idx, "big", "", 3)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Contains(t, out, "truncated")
	// Should have at most 3 source lines + 1 truncation note.
	require.Equal(t, 4, lineCount(out))
}

func TestGetFunctionSource_FilePathHint(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	a := `package main

func hello() string { return "a" }
`
	b := `package main

func hello() string { return "b" }
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "a.go"), []byte(a), 0o600))
	require.NoError(t, os.MkdirAll(filepath.Join(tmp, "sub"), 0o750))
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "sub", "b.go"), []byte(b), 0o600))

	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetFunctionSource(idx, "hello", "sub/b.go", 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Contains(t, out, `return "b"`)
}

func lineCount(s string) int {
	n := 0
	for _, c := range s {
		if c == '\n' {
			n++
		}
	}
	if len(s) > 0 && s[len(s)-1] != '\n' {
		n++
	}
	return n
}
```

```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetFunctionSource -v
```
Expected: FAIL — `undefined: GetFunctionSource`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement source.go**

Create `internal/query/source.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"

	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// GetFunctionSource returns the source of a function/method by qualified name.
//
// filePath is an optional disambiguator: when non-empty and the index has
// a matching symbol in that file, prefer that file. When empty, the index's
// SymbolTable entry is used (first-seen wins on collisions).
//
// maxLines > 0 truncates the output at maxLines and appends a note.
//
// Returns the source text on success, or a human-readable "Error: …" /
// "Symbol 'X' not found" string. The error return is reserved for I/O
// failures (file removed under us); name-not-found is not an error.
func GetFunctionSource(idx *models.ProjectIndex, name, filePath string, maxLines int) (string, error) {
	fn, path, ok := findFunctionByQualified(idx, name, filePath)
	if !ok {
		return fmt.Sprintf("Symbol %q not found", name), nil
	}
	body, err := readFileLines(filepath.Join(idx.Root, path), fn.Line, fn.EndLine)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	if maxLines > 0 {
		lines := strings.Split(body, "\n")
		if len(lines) > maxLines {
			lines = lines[:maxLines]
			lines = append(lines, "... (truncated; pass max_lines=N to expand)")
			body = strings.Join(lines, "\n")
		}
	}
	return body, nil
}

// findFunctionByQualified locates a function across all files by qualified
// name. When filePath is non-empty and contains a matching symbol, that file
// is preferred. Returns (function, file path, found).
func findFunctionByQualified(idx *models.ProjectIndex, qualified, filePath string) (models.Function, string, bool) {
	if filePath != "" {
		if md, ok := idx.Files[filePath]; ok {
			for _, f := range md.Functions {
				if f.Qualified == qualified || f.Name == qualified {
					return f, filePath, true
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if path, ok := idx.SymbolTable[qualified]; ok {
		if md, ok := idx.Files[path]; ok {
			for _, f := range md.Functions {
				if f.Qualified == qualified {
					return f, path, true
				}
			}
		}
	}
	// Fall back to full scan — handles `name` -> `Class.name` lookups.
	for _, p := range idx.SortedPaths {
		md := idx.Files[p]
		for _, f := range md.Functions {
			if f.Qualified == qualified || f.Name == qualified {
				return f, p, true
			}
		}
	}
	return models.Function{}, "", false
}

// readFileLines returns the substring of path's contents between startLine
// and endLine inclusive (1-based). EOF before endLine is tolerated.
func readFileLines(path string, startLine, endLine int) (string, error) {
	raw, err := os.ReadFile(path)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	if startLine < 1 {
		startLine = 1
	}
	lines := strings.Split(string(raw), "\n")
	if startLine > len(lines) {
		return "", nil
	}
	if endLine > len(lines) {
		endLine = len(lines)
	}
	return strings.Join(lines[startLine-1:endLine], "\n"), nil
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetFunctionSource -v
```
Expected: PASS for all four tests.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash
git add internal/query/source.go internal/query/source_test.go
git commit -m "feat(query): add GetFunctionSource

Resolves qualified name to (file, line, end_line) via the index, reads
the file from disk, slices the body. filePath hint disambiguates
collisions; max_lines>0 truncates with a hint. Symbol-not-found returns
a human-readable string (matches Python — name-not-found is not an
error condition)."
```

## Task 26: get_class_source

**Files:**
- Create: addition to `internal/query/source.go`, `internal/query/source_test.go`

Mirrors `GetFunctionSource` but resolves through the index's class list. Includes Python's auto-downgrade behaviour: when `max_lines == 0` (caller took the default) AND the class body exceeds 300 lines, auto-downgrade to a method-signature summary and append a hint. The L2 summary is `class Foo:` followed by an indented bullet per method signature.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test**

Append to `internal/query/source_test.go`:
```go
func TestGetClassSource_Found(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

type Greeter struct {
	name string
}

func (g *Greeter) Hello() string { return "hi " + g.name }
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetClassSource(idx, "Greeter", "", 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Contains(t, out, "type Greeter struct")
}

func TestGetClassSource_NotFound(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte("package main\n"), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetClassSource(idx, "Missing", "", 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Contains(t, out, "not found")
}

func TestGetClassSource_AutoDowngradeForLargeClass(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	var b strings.Builder
	b.WriteString("package main\n\ntype Big struct {\n")
	for i := 0; i < 320; i++ {
		b.WriteString("\tx int\n")
	}
	b.WriteString("}\n")
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(b.String()), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetClassSource(idx, "Big", "", 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Contains(t, out, "class too large")
}

func TestGetClassSource_ExplicitMaxLinesBypassesAutoDowngrade(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	var b strings.Builder
	b.WriteString("package main\n\ntype Big struct {\n")
	for i := 0; i < 320; i++ {
		b.WriteString("\tx int\n")
	}
	b.WriteString("}\n")
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(b.String()), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetClassSource(idx, "Big", "", 500)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.NotContains(t, out, "class too large")
}
```

Add `"strings"` to test imports if not present.

- [ ] **Step 2: Run the test to verify it fails**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetClassSource -v
```
Expected: FAIL — `undefined: GetClassSource`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement GetClassSource**

Append to `internal/query/source.go`:
```go
// GetClassSource returns the source of a class/type by qualified name.
//
// Auto-downgrade rule (matches Python query_api.py:1073): when maxLines == 0
// (caller took the default) AND the body exceeds 300 lines, emit a
// method-signature summary instead and prepend a `[class too large -- N
// lines. Showing L2 summary; pass max_lines=N for raw source.]` line.
// Explicit non-zero maxLines bypasses this.
func GetClassSource(idx *models.ProjectIndex, name, filePath string, maxLines int) (string, error) {
	cls, path, ok := findClassByQualified(idx, name, filePath)
	if !ok {
		return fmt.Sprintf("Symbol %q not found", name), nil
	}
	body, err := readFileLines(filepath.Join(idx.Root, path), cls.Line, cls.EndLine)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	lineN := strings.Count(body, "\n") + 1
	if maxLines == 0 && lineN > 300 {
		summary := classMethodSummary(idx, name, path)
		head := fmt.Sprintf("[class too large -- %d lines. Showing L2 summary; pass max_lines=N for raw source.]\n", lineN)
		return head + summary, nil
	}
	if maxLines > 0 {
		lines := strings.Split(body, "\n")
		if len(lines) > maxLines {
			lines = lines[:maxLines]
			lines = append(lines, "... (truncated; pass max_lines=N to expand)")
			body = strings.Join(lines, "\n")
		}
	}
	return body, nil
}

// findClassByQualified is the class-side mirror of findFunctionByQualified.
func findClassByQualified(idx *models.ProjectIndex, qualified, filePath string) (models.Class, string, bool) {
	if filePath != "" {
		if md, ok := idx.Files[filePath]; ok {
			for _, c := range md.Classes {
				if c.Qualified == qualified || c.Name == qualified {
					return c, filePath, true
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if path, ok := idx.SymbolTable[qualified]; ok {
		if md, ok := idx.Files[path]; ok {
			for _, c := range md.Classes {
				if c.Qualified == qualified {
					return c, path, true
				}
			}
		}
	}
	for _, p := range idx.SortedPaths {
		md := idx.Files[p]
		for _, c := range md.Classes {
			if c.Qualified == qualified || c.Name == qualified {
				return c, p, true
			}
		}
	}
	return models.Class{}, "", false
}

// classMethodSummary returns a compact list of the class's method signatures.
// Format: "class Name:\n  - sig\n  - sig\n". Methods are identified by
// Receiver = class name.
func classMethodSummary(idx *models.ProjectIndex, className, path string) string {
	md, ok := idx.Files[path]
	if !ok {
		return fmt.Sprintf("class %s:\n  (no methods found)\n", className)
	}
	var b strings.Builder
	fmt.Fprintf(&b, "class %s:\n", className)
	for _, f := range md.Functions {
		if f.Receiver != className {
			continue
		}
		sig := f.Signature
		if sig == "" {
			sig = f.Name + "(...)"
		}
		fmt.Fprintf(&b, "  - %s\n", sig)
	}
	return b.String()
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetClassSource -v
```
Expected: PASS for all four tests.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash
git add internal/query/source.go internal/query/source_test.go
git commit -m "feat(query): add GetClassSource with auto-downgrade for large classes

Mirror of GetFunctionSource on the class side. When maxLines==0 (caller
took the default) AND body exceeds 300 lines, emit a method-signature
summary (L2 in Python's nomenclature) and append a hint pointing at the
max_lines override. Explicit maxLines bypasses the auto-downgrade.
Matches Python query_api.py:1073 behaviour."
```

## Task 27: get_dependents (reverse-graph walk)

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/query/dependents.go`, `internal/query/dependents_test.go`

`DepGraph` is `caller → callees`. The reverse view (`callee → callers`) is computed on demand: scan every entry of `DepGraph`, invert.

Python signature: `get_dependents(name, max_results=0, max_total_chars=50_000)`. Returns a `list[dict]` with `{file, line, qualified, …}` per caller, followed by a sentinel `{"_complete": true, "total": N}` when not truncated, or a `{"truncated": true, "message": …}` when char-cap hit.

For the Go wire shape we keep the same identity (`file`, `line`, `qualified`) and let `expected_diffs.go` normalize Python's per-symbol-info shape to ours.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test**

Create `internal/query/dependents_test.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

	_ "token-savior-go/internal/annotator/golang"
	"token-savior-go/internal/indexer"
)

func TestGetDependents_DirectCallers(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func helper() {}

func a() { helper() }
func b() { helper() }
func c() { other() }
func other() {}
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetDependents(idx, "helper", 0, 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	// Two dependents (a, b) + the _complete sentinel.
	require.GreaterOrEqual(t, len(out), 2)

	qualifieds := dependentQualifieds(out)
	require.Contains(t, qualifieds, "a")
	require.Contains(t, qualifieds, "b")
	require.NotContains(t, qualifieds, "c")
}

func TestGetDependents_NotInGraph(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte("package main\n"), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetDependents(idx, "MissingFn", 0, 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Len(t, out, 1)
	require.NotNil(t, out[0]["error"])
}

func TestGetDependents_MaxResultsTruncates(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func helper() {}

func a() { helper() }
func b() { helper() }
func c() { helper() }
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetDependents(idx, "helper", 2, 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	// Exactly 2 dependents — no _complete sentinel because we truncated.
	q := dependentQualifieds(out)
	require.Len(t, q, 2)
}

func dependentQualifieds(out []map[string]any) []string {
	var q []string
	for _, m := range out {
		if v, ok := m["qualified"].(string); ok {
			q = append(q, v)
		}
	}
	return q
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Run the test to verify it fails**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetDependents -v
```
Expected: FAIL — `undefined: GetDependents`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement dependents.go**

Create `internal/query/dependents.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"sort"

	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// GetDependents returns the callers of name from the dep graph.
//
// maxResults > 0 caps the number of caller entries.
// maxTotalChars > 0 caps the cumulative JSON-encoded size; when hit, we stop
// adding entries and append a single {truncated:true, message:…} sentinel.
//
// Return shape (slice of map[string]any so the dispatcher can JSON-encode
// without an extra struct):
//   [
//     {"qualified": "...", "file": "...", "line": N, "kind": "function"|"class"},
//     ...,
//     {"_complete": true, "total": N}        // appended when no truncation
//   ]
//
// On unknown name: single-entry list with {"error": "..."}.
func GetDependents(idx *models.ProjectIndex, name string, maxResults, maxTotalChars int) ([]map[string]any, error) {
	callers := buildReverseEdges(idx)[name]
	if callers == nil {
		// Not in the reverse graph — either name doesn't exist or no one calls it.
		// Check the symbol table; if name is known but has no callers, return an
		// empty result with _complete; otherwise error.
		if _, known := idx.SymbolTable[name]; !known {
			return []map[string]any{{"error": fmt.Sprintf("'%s' not found in reverse dependency graph", name)}}, nil
		}
		return []map[string]any{{"_complete": true, "total": 0}}, nil
	}
	sorted := make([]string, 0, len(callers))
	for k := range callers {
		sorted = append(sorted, k)
	}
	sort.Strings(sorted)
	total := len(sorted)
	if maxResults > 0 && len(sorted) > maxResults {
		sorted = sorted[:maxResults]
	}
	var out []map[string]any
	charsUsed := 0
	truncated := false
	for _, dep := range sorted {
		entry := resolveSymbolInfo(idx, dep)
		if maxTotalChars > 0 {
			raw, _ := json.Marshal(entry)
			if charsUsed+len(raw) > maxTotalChars {
				out = append(out, map[string]any{
					"truncated": true,
					"message":   fmt.Sprintf("... output truncated at %d chars. Use max_results to narrow the scope.", maxTotalChars),
					"shown":     len(out),
					"total":     total,
				})
				truncated = true
				break
			}
			charsUsed += len(raw)
		}
		out = append(out, entry)
	}
	if !truncated && (maxResults == 0 || len(out) == total) {
		out = append(out, map[string]any{"_complete": true, "total": total})
	}
	return out, nil
}

// buildReverseEdges inverts the index's DepGraph in O(N) time.
// Returns callee -> set of callers.
func buildReverseEdges(idx *models.ProjectIndex) map[string]map[string]struct{} {
	rev := make(map[string]map[string]struct{}, len(idx.DepGraph))
	for caller, callees := range idx.DepGraph {
		for callee := range callees {
			if rev[callee] == nil {
				rev[callee] = make(map[string]struct{})
			}
			rev[callee][caller] = struct{}{}
		}
	}
	return rev
}

// resolveSymbolInfo returns {qualified, file, line, kind} for a known
// symbol, or {qualified, file: "", line: 0} for an unresolved name.
func resolveSymbolInfo(idx *models.ProjectIndex, name string) map[string]any {
	out := map[string]any{"qualified": name}
	path, ok := idx.SymbolTable[name]
	if !ok {
		out["file"] = ""
		out["line"] = 0
		return out
	}
	md, ok := idx.Files[path]
	if !ok {
		out["file"] = path
		out["line"] = 0
		return out
	}
	for _, f := range md.Functions {
		if f.Qualified == name {
			out["file"] = path
			out["line"] = f.Line
			out["end_line"] = f.EndLine
			out["kind"] = "function"
			return out
		}
	}
	for _, c := range md.Classes {
		if c.Qualified == name {
			out["file"] = path
			out["line"] = c.Line
			out["end_line"] = c.EndLine
			out["kind"] = "class"
			return out
		}
	}
	out["file"] = path
	out["line"] = 0
	return out
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetDependents -v
```
Expected: PASS for all three tests.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash

git commit -m "feat(query): add GetDependents (reverse-graph walker)

Inverts DepGraph in O(N), sorts callers lexicographically, applies
max_results and max_total_chars caps. Appends a {_complete: true,
total: N} sentinel when no truncation; otherwise a {truncated: true,
message: ...}. Unknown name returns a single-entry [{error: ...}]
slice to match Python's wire shape."
```

## Task 28: get_dependencies (forward-graph walker, with BFS)

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/query/dependencies.go`, `internal/query/dependencies_test.go`

Forward direction: given `name`, return what it calls. `depth=1` is direct deps only; `depth>1` does BFS up to that depth with cycle protection.

Python signature: `get_dependencies(name, max_results=0, depth=1)`.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test**

Create `internal/query/dependencies_test.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

	_ "token-savior-go/internal/annotator/golang"
	"token-savior-go/internal/indexer"
)

func TestGetDependencies_Direct(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func leaf1() {}
func leaf2() {}

func mid() {
	leaf1()
	leaf2()
}

func root() {
	mid()
}
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetDependencies(idx, "mid", 0, 1)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	q := depQualifieds(out)
	require.Contains(t, q, "leaf1")
	require.Contains(t, q, "leaf2")
	require.NotContains(t, q, "root") // not a dep — root depends ON mid, not the other way around.
}

func TestGetDependencies_TransitiveDepth2(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func leaf() {}

func mid() { leaf() }
func root() { mid() }
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetDependencies(idx, "root", 0, 2)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	q := depQualifieds(out)
	require.Contains(t, q, "mid")
	require.Contains(t, q, "leaf")
}

func TestGetDependencies_CycleProtection(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func a() { b() }
func b() { a() }
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetDependencies(idx, "a", 0, 5)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	// Should terminate; output should include b but not loop infinitely.
	q := depQualifieds(out)
	require.Contains(t, q, "b")
}

func TestGetDependencies_NotFound(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte("package main\n"), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetDependencies(idx, "Missing", 0, 1)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Len(t, out, 1)
	require.NotNil(t, out[0]["error"])
}

func depQualifieds(out []map[string]any) []string {
	var q []string
	for _, m := range out {
		if v, ok := m["qualified"].(string); ok {
			q = append(q, v)
		}
	}
	return q
}
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement dependencies.go**

Create `internal/query/dependencies.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"fmt"
	"sort"

	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// GetDependencies returns the symbols that name calls (or transitively calls,
// when depth > 1). Cycles are skipped via a visited set.
//
// Return shape mirrors GetDependents: slice of maps with {qualified, file,
// line, kind, [depth]}, plus a trailing {_complete: true, total: N, [depth_reached: N]}
// when the full set was walked.
//
// On unknown name: single-entry list with {error: ...}.
func GetDependencies(idx *models.ProjectIndex, name string, maxResults, depth int) ([]map[string]any, error) {
	if _, known := idx.DepGraph[name]; !known {
		// Maybe a symbol but with no outgoing edges — distinguish.
		if _, inSym := idx.SymbolTable[name]; !inSym {
			return []map[string]any{{"error": fmt.Sprintf("'%s' not found in dependency graph", name)}}, nil
		}
	}
	if depth <= 1 {
		deps := idx.DepGraph[name]
		sorted := setToSortedSlice(deps)
		total := len(sorted)
		if maxResults > 0 && len(sorted) > maxResults {
			sorted = sorted[:maxResults]
		}
		out := make([]map[string]any, 0, len(sorted)+1)
		for _, d := range sorted {
			out = append(out, resolveSymbolInfo(idx, d))
		}
		if maxResults == 0 || len(out) == total {
			out = append(out, map[string]any{"_complete": true, "total": total})
		}
		return out, nil
	}
	// BFS depth > 1.
	seen := map[string]bool{name: true}
	var out []map[string]any
	frontier := []string{name}
	hitCap := false
	for layer := 1; layer <= depth; layer++ {
		var next []string
		for _, node := range frontier {
			deps := setToSortedSlice(idx.DepGraph[node])
			for _, dep := range deps {
				if seen[dep] {
					continue
				}
				seen[dep] = true
				info := resolveSymbolInfo(idx, dep)
				info["depth"] = layer
				info["from"] = node
				out = append(out, info)
				next = append(next, dep)
				if maxResults > 0 && len(out) >= maxResults {
					hitCap = true
					break
				}
			}
			if hitCap {
				break
			}
		}
		if hitCap {
			break
		}
		frontier = next
		if len(frontier) == 0 {
			break
		}
	}
	if !hitCap {
		out = append(out, map[string]any{"_complete": true, "total": len(out), "depth_reached": depth})
	}
	return out, nil
}

func setToSortedSlice(s map[string]struct{}) []string {
	out := make([]string, 0, len(s))
	for k := range s {
		out = append(out, k)
	}
	sort.Strings(out)
	return out
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests**

Run:
```bash

```
Expected: PASS for all four tests.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash
git commit -m "feat(query): add GetDependencies (forward-graph walker with BFS)

depth=1: direct deps only. depth>1: BFS with seen-set cycle protection;
each entry tags depth and from. max_results truncates anywhere in the
walk. Unknown name returns [{error: …}] to match Python's shape."
```

## Task 29: get_change_impact

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/query/impact.go`, `internal/query/impact_test.go`

Direct + transitive dependents, each tagged with `confidence = max(0.05, 0.6^(depth-1))` and `depth`. Splits the output into two arrays `direct` and `transitive`, sorted by descending confidence, with a global `max_total_chars` cap that trims transitive first, then direct.

Python signature: `get_change_impact(name, max_direct=0, max_transitive=0, max_total_chars=50_000)`. Reference: `src/token_savior/query_api.py:1630`.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test**

Create `internal/query/impact_test.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

	_ "token-savior-go/internal/annotator/golang"
	"token-savior-go/internal/indexer"
)

func TestGetChangeImpact_DirectAndTransitive(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func leaf() {}
func mid() { leaf() }
func root() { mid() }
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetChangeImpact(idx, "leaf", 0, 0, 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	direct, _ := out["direct"].([]map[string]any)
	transitive, _ := out["transitive"].([]map[string]any)

	directQ := mapSlice(direct, "qualified")
	transQ := mapSlice(transitive, "qualified")
	require.Contains(t, directQ, "mid")
	require.Contains(t, transQ, "root")
}

func TestGetChangeImpact_ConfidenceDecay(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func leaf() {}
func d1() { leaf() }
func d2() { d1() }
func d3() { d2() }
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetChangeImpact(idx, "leaf", 0, 0, 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	direct, _ := out["direct"].([]map[string]any)
	for _, e := range direct {
		require.InDelta(t, 1.0, e["confidence"], 0.001) // 0.6^0 == 1.0
		require.Equal(t, 1, e["depth"])
	}
	transitive, _ := out["transitive"].([]map[string]any)
	// Confidence sorted descending.
	if len(transitive) >= 2 {
		c0 := transitive[0]["confidence"].(float64)
		c1 := transitive[1]["confidence"].(float64)
		require.GreaterOrEqual(t, c0, c1)
	}
}

func TestGetChangeImpact_NotFound(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte("package main\n"), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetChangeImpact(idx, "Missing", 0, 0, 0)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.NotNil(t, out["error"])
}

func mapSlice(ms []map[string]any, key string) []string {
	var out []string
	for _, m := range ms {
		if v, ok := m[key].(string); ok {
			out = append(out, v)
		}
	}
	return out
}
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Run the test to verify it fails**

```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetChangeImpact -v
```
Expected: FAIL — `undefined: GetChangeImpact`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement impact.go**

Create `internal/query/impact.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"math"
	"sort"

	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// GetChangeImpact returns the impact tree for a symbol: direct dependents
// (depth 1) plus transitive dependents (depth >= 2), each annotated with
// confidence = max(0.05, 0.6^(depth-1)). Sorts each list by descending
// confidence. Trims transitive first, then direct, to fit max_total_chars.
//
// Unknown name returns {"error": "..."}.
func GetChangeImpact(idx *models.ProjectIndex, name string, maxDirect, maxTransitive, maxTotalChars int) (map[string]any, error) {
	rev := buildReverseEdges(idx)
	direct, found := rev[name]
	if !found {
		if _, known := idx.SymbolTable[name]; !known {
			return map[string]any{"error": fmt.Sprintf("'%s' not found in reverse dependency graph", name)}, nil
		}
		direct = map[string]struct{}{}
	}

	// BFS for depth tracking.
	depthMap := make(map[string]int)
	queue := make([]queueEntry, 0, len(direct))
	visited := make(map[string]bool)
	for sym := range direct {
		depthMap[sym] = 1
		queue = append(queue, queueEntry{sym, 1})
		visited[sym] = true
	}
	for len(queue) > 0 {
		cur := queue[0]
		queue = queue[1:]
		for next := range rev[cur.name] {
			if visited[next] {
				continue
			}
			visited[next] = true
			depthMap[next] = cur.depth + 1
			queue = append(queue, queueEntry{next, cur.depth + 1})
		}
	}

	// Build entries.
	makeEntry := func(sym string) map[string]any {
		d := depthMap[sym]
		conf := math.Max(0.05, math.Pow(0.6, float64(d-1)))
		info := resolveSymbolInfo(idx, sym)
		info["confidence"] = conf
		info["depth"] = d
		return info
	}

	directEntries := make([]map[string]any, 0, len(direct))
	for sym := range direct {
		directEntries = append(directEntries, makeEntry(sym))
	}
	sortByConfidenceDesc(directEntries)
	if maxDirect > 0 && len(directEntries) > maxDirect {
		directEntries = directEntries[:maxDirect]
	}

	transitiveEntries := make([]map[string]any, 0)
	for sym := range depthMap {
		if _, isDirect := direct[sym]; isDirect {
			continue
		}
		transitiveEntries = append(transitiveEntries, makeEntry(sym))
	}
	sortByConfidenceDesc(transitiveEntries)
	if maxTransitive > 0 && len(transitiveEntries) > maxTransitive {
		transitiveEntries = transitiveEntries[:maxTransitive]
	}

	result := map[string]any{
		"direct":     directEntries,
		"transitive": transitiveEntries,
	}

	if maxTotalChars > 0 {
		for len(transitiveEntries) > 0 && jsonLen(result) > maxTotalChars {
			transitiveEntries = transitiveEntries[:len(transitiveEntries)-1]
			result["transitive"] = transitiveEntries
		}
		for len(directEntries) > 0 && jsonLen(result) > maxTotalChars {
			directEntries = directEntries[:len(directEntries)-1]
			result["direct"] = directEntries
		}
		if jsonLen(result) > maxTotalChars {
			result["truncated"] = true
			result["message"] = fmt.Sprintf("... output truncated at %d chars. Use max_direct / max_transitive to narrow the scope.", maxTotalChars)
		}
	}

	return result, nil
}

type queueEntry struct {
	name  string
	depth int
}

func sortByConfidenceDesc(entries []map[string]any) {
	sort.SliceStable(entries, func(i, j int) bool {
		ci, _ := entries[i]["confidence"].(float64)
		cj, _ := entries[j]["confidence"].(float64)
		return ci > cj
	})
}

func jsonLen(v any) int {
	raw, _ := json.Marshal(v)
	return len(raw)
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetChangeImpact -v
```
Expected: PASS for all three.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash
git add internal/query/impact.go internal/query/impact_test.go
git commit -m "feat(query): add GetChangeImpact (BFS with confidence decay)

Direct + transitive dependents, each annotated confidence = max(0.05,
0.6^(depth-1)) and depth = BFS layer. Sorts each list by descending
confidence. max_total_chars trims transitive first, then direct, then
sets truncated=true with a hint. Matches Python query_api.py:1630."
```

## Task 30: get_call_chain (shortest-path BFS)

**Files:**
- Create: `internal/query/chain.go`, `internal/query/chain_test.go`

Shortest path in the dep graph from `from_name` to `to_name`. BFS over `DepGraph` (forward direction). When `from == to`, return a one-element chain. When no path exists, return `{error: "..."}`.

Python signature: `get_call_chain(from_name, to_name, level=2)`. We ignore `level` for M2 (just return the chain) — it's a hop-verbosity knob that's M5+ work.

Return shape: `{"chain": [info1, info2, …]}` where each `info` is a `resolveSymbolInfo` map.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test**

Create `internal/query/chain_test.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

	_ "token-savior-go/internal/annotator/golang"
	"token-savior-go/internal/indexer"
)

func TestGetCallChain_DirectPath(t *testing.T) {
	tmp := t.TempDir()
	src := `package main

func leaf() {}
func mid() { leaf() }
func root() { mid() }
`
	require.NoError(t, os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(tmp, "main.go"), []byte(src), 0o600))
	idx, _ := indexer.NewProjectIndexer(tmp).Build()

	out, err := GetCallChain(idx, "root", "leaf")
	require.NoError(t, err)
	chain, ok := out["chain"].([]map[string]any)
	require.True(t, ok)
	require.Equal(t, 3, len(chain))
	require.Equal(t, "root", chain[0]["qualified"])
	require.Equal(t, "mid", chain[1]["qualified"])
	require.Equal(t, "leaf", chain[2]["qualified"])

	require.Equal(t, "solo", chain[0]["qualified"])
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Run the test to verify it fails**

```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetCallChain -v
```
Expected: FAIL — `undefined: GetCallChain`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Implement chain.go**

Create `internal/query/chain.go`:
```go
package query

import (
	"fmt"
	"sort"

	"token-savior-go/internal/models"
)

// GetCallChain returns the shortest path in the dep graph from fromName to
// toName via BFS over forward edges (DepGraph[caller] -> callees).
//
// Returns:
//   {"chain": [info1, info2, …]}  on success (each info is a symbol map)
//   {"error": "..."}              when either endpoint isn't known or no path
//
// Same-symbol short-circuit (from == to) returns a one-element chain.
func GetCallChain(idx *models.ProjectIndex, fromName, toName string) (map[string]any, error) {
	if _, ok := idx.SymbolTable[fromName]; !ok {
		if _, ok := idx.DepGraph[fromName]; !ok {
			return map[string]any{"error": fmt.Sprintf("'%s' not found in dependency graph", fromName)}, nil
		}
	}
	if _, ok := idx.SymbolTable[toName]; !ok {
		// Allow toName to be an unresolved callee (we still have edges TO it).
		if !hasIncomingEdge(idx, toName) {
			return map[string]any{"error": fmt.Sprintf("'%s' not found in dependency graph", toName)}, nil
		}
	}
	if fromName == toName {
		info := resolveSymbolInfo(idx, fromName)
		return map[string]any{"chain": []map[string]any{info}}, nil
	}

	// BFS.
	visited := map[string]bool{fromName: true}
	parents := map[string]string{}
	queue := []string{fromName}
	found := false
	for len(queue) > 0 && !found {
		cur := queue[0]
		queue = queue[1:]
		neighbors := setToSortedSlice(idx.DepGraph[cur])
		for _, nb := range neighbors {
			if visited[nb] {
				continue
			}
			visited[nb] = true
			parents[nb] = cur
			if nb == toName {
				found = true
				break
			}
			queue = append(queue, nb)
		}
	}
	if !found {
		return map[string]any{"error": fmt.Sprintf("no path from '%s' to '%s'", fromName, toName)}, nil
	}
	// Reconstruct.
	var pathNames []string
	for cur := toName; cur != ""; {
		pathNames = append([]string{cur}, pathNames...)
		if cur == fromName {
			break
		}
		cur = parents[cur]
	}
	chain := make([]map[string]any, 0, len(pathNames))
	for _, n := range pathNames {
		chain = append(chain, resolveSymbolInfo(idx, n))
	}
	return map[string]any{"chain": chain}, nil
}

// hasIncomingEdge returns true if any caller has an edge to name.
func hasIncomingEdge(idx *models.ProjectIndex, name string) bool {
	for _, callees := range idx.DepGraph {
		if _, ok := callees[name]; ok {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}

// (compile-time use to keep sort imported in this file if needed)
var _ = sort.Strings
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests**

Run:
```bash
go test ./internal/query/ -run TestGetCallChain -v
```
Expected: PASS for all four.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash
git add internal/query/chain.go internal/query/chain_test.go
git commit -m "feat(query): add GetCallChain (BFS shortest path on DepGraph)

Sorts neighbours lexicographically so the chain is deterministic across
runs. Same-symbol case returns a one-element chain. Unknown endpoint
returns {error: ...}. Hop-verbosity 'level' parameter from Python is
not modelled in M2 — accept the parity gap, document in
expected_diffs.go if the harness flags it."
```
